Foreign Important Telegrams

German Chancellor Declares Inability to Bear Reparations 73

Causes Shock in Paris

French Finance Minister Flandin Publishes Article Claiming Sacred Contracts Cannot Be Broken

▲Reuters, Berlin, 9th: German Chancellor Brüning told the British ambassador yesterday that Germany would demand the cancellation of reparations at the reparations conference. Today, he issued another article stating that it is impossible for Germany to continue paying political reparations. He believes that no one today is unaware of the inevitable consequences. Now, we must muster courage and not allow economic problems to be subject to political considerations. The Basel Conference report has shown the tragic consequences of the war suffered by Germany and acknowledged the extreme measures taken by Germany to resist its difficulties, which are unprecedented in modern history. This report also shows that Germany's plan alone is of no avail. World financial difficulties are increasing, and the reasons for this are mostly Germany's position. Therefore, Germany must earnestly request that all governments immediately take joint action. Brüning also said that Germany's inability to pay its debts, the close relationship between German reparations and the world situation, and the circumstances under which the Young Plan was established have now undergone a thorough change, as proven by the Basel Conference report. The continuation of German political reparations is impossible for Germany's situation. If there is a scheme to maintain this reparation, it will inevitably cause a dramatic disaster not only for Germany but also for the entire world. Germany agreed to the proposal put forward by France and supported by Britain to hold the Lausanne Reparations Conference on January 25. The German government has no other choice in the attitude and events it can adopt. There is no other way but to state the truth at the conference and ask other governments concerned to consider the current situation and not try to mediate, because this possibility no longer exists.

▲Reuters, Paris, 9th: Brüning's remarks have caused shock in Paris. Members of the parliament today unanimously recognized the seriousness of this development. Most people say that Germany is determined to deny its obligations under the Young Plan, making the Lausanne Reparations Conference a useless move. The creditor nations should immediately consult on a common attitude. The Young Plan stipulates that if Germany defaults, it can appeal to the International Court of Justice in The Hague. People in political circles all say that in the German Chancellor's move, they can see the hand of Hitler, the leader of the National Socialist Party. Finance Minister Flandin published an article, saying that if Brüning's remarks are true as reported, it means that the German government wants to cancel the Young Plan and the Treaty of Versailles. The French people will never allow it to be unilaterally cancelled and destroy France's sacred right to reparations. No one denies the severity of the world's panic and the need to revise the government's payment methods in order to overcome the difficulties. The French government is currently working on this matter and is studying a plan that creditors and debtors can agree on with a very moderate spirit to alleviate the difficulties. But if a new attack is launched on the contract, causing the difficulties to become more entangled, it will only make this difficulty insurmountable. The only result of this move is to make it even more impossible for people to invest.

▲National News Agency, Berlin, 9th: Yesterday, Brüning told the British ambassador that Germany was unable to pay reparations again. Therefore, the German Foreign Ministry in Berlin immediately denied the foreign reports that Mr. Bai had spoken to the British ambassador. However, those who are well-informed believe that what the German Foreign Ministry denied was only the wording of the British record of the conversation. As for the fact that Mr. Bai had asked the British ambassador to pay attention to Germany's inability to raise funds to pay reparations, it is undoubtedly true. Not long after, Mr. Bai did have a conversation with the press.

Havas, Berlin, 9th: According to political circles, Brüning did not declare to the British ambassador that Germany would no longer pay compensation, as foreign newspapers reported. Mr. Bai met with the British ambassador for a long time and only said that, according to Germany's situation, it is really impossible to pay compensation at this time, and it is feared that there will be no power to pay in the future. According to the opinion of German people, Brüning's declaration is not as absolute as foreign telegrams reported, and it is said that the German government will decide its attitude on this matter within the shortest possible time.

Reuters, New York, 9th: The New York banking community was not alarmed today by the German Chancellor's declaration that Germany could no longer pay reparations. A prominent banker said that the original intention of this declaration was to feign hope in order to facilitate negotiations. He expects that a payment method can always be agreed upon in the future. Even if the Allied powers refuse to pay their war debts to the United States, it will not cause great distress to the United States, because once the debt problem is resolved, trade can be quickly revived, and what the United States can gain in prosperous trade will be many times the amount of the debt.

Colonel Roosevelt to Succeed Him

▲National News Agency, Washington, 9th: Philippine Governor Davis, who is currently on leave in the United States, officially resigned today. The US President transferred Colonel Roosevelt, the Governor of Puerto Rico, to succeed him as the Governor of the Philippine Islands. The order has been issued, and Roosevelt is currently in Washington and is said to be going to the Philippines to take office soon. (Continued by Reuters) Roosevelt is the son of the former president, 44 years old. In recent years, he has traveled to the East twice. He served on the front lines during the war and received medals from the US and French governments. He was the Undersecretary of the Navy from 1921 to 1924.

Foreign Important Telegrams 2

US Naval Maneuvers to Begin on the Opening Day of the Disarmament Conference 75

Fleet Assembled in the Pacific

109,000 Participants

1,200 Aircraft

Battle Line Reaches the Philippine Islands

A Major Threat to Japan

National News Agency, Washington, 9th: The Naval Department announced today that the US battle fleet will depart from various Pacific ports for Hawaii on February 6. The US battle fleet's annual winter maneuvers are planned to be held in Hawaiian waters this year.

New York News: Regarding the Pacific maneuvers of the entire US Navy, the US Navy magazine Navy has detailed records, stating that the maneuver plan includes three aircraft carriers, eighteen battleships, nineteen cruisers, two hundred and thirty-three destroyers, and one hundred and seven submarines. 109,000 naval personnel and the entire air force will participate, with a number of up to 1,200 aircraft. The maneuver dates are scheduled to begin on February 1 and end in mid-May. The maneuvers will be centered around the island of Honolulu, with joint land and sea maneuvers held in the areas of San Francisco and Seattle. The battle line extends from the east coast of the United States to the Philippine Islands. The Atlantic side is scheduled to depart in full force on the 20th of this month. A large-scale simulated battle is planned on the Panama Canal, with the air force bombing the canal to prevent the passage of the Atlantic fleet. The fleet side plans to use anti-aircraft guns to defend its advance. As for the location of the first stage of the maneuvers, it is on the island of Honolulu. The enemy ships attacking the island of Honolulu will be fiercely attacked from the air, sea, and underwater, in coordination with the land and sea forces defending the island of Honolulu to destroy the enemy forces. The third stage of the maneuvers is centered on the west coast of the United States. The entire Atlantic fleet will protect the coast of more than 10,000 nautical miles. The third stage of the maneuvers is a major battle on the entire Pacific Ocean, with the entire aircraft, warships, and submarines dispatched. (World News Agency)

Two Major Parties in the United States Decide on Dates for Conventions 78

To Elect Presidential Candidates

Dawes Has No Intention of Joining the Election Campaign

National News Agency, Washington, 9th: The Democratic National Committee gathered here today and resolved to convene the Democratic National Convention in Chicago on June 27 this year to elect presidential and vice-presidential candidates. Many members of the Democratic Party now advocate opening up the ban on alcohol and will use this as one of the campaign platforms, believing that it can reduce the number of unemployed and cause disturbances due to economic and financial decline.

▲Reuters, Washington, 6th: US Dawes resigned from his post as Ambassador to the United Kingdom. It is said that Dawes once served as Vice President and now leaves his official position, perhaps wanting to compete in the next presidential election. Today, someone raised this question with Dawes, who said it was nonsense. As soon as this statement was made, the rumors ceased.

Japanese in Osaka Brutally Assault Chinese Merchants 79

Two Injured, Two Thrown into the Water

Osaka News: Zhou Bujin and others, the owners of Yuanyuan Company, a Chinese merchant in Osaka, encountered several Japanese people, including one named Lin, demanding land rent on the way, leading to an argument. At that time, dozens of Japanese passers-by joined the attack, wielding clubs and canes. Zhou and Li Zhilin were injured in the head and other places and were treated at Kitagawa Hospital. Two other overseas Chinese were thrown into the Shirinengawa River (commonly known as Matsushima Canal). When they came out of the water, their clothes and shoes were completely wet. Later, Japanese police rushed to the scene, but the attacking Japanese had scattered and fled. (World News Agency)

Important News

The Japanese Army in Yuguan Provokes but Fails 80

Shanhaiguan Correspondence: The Japanese army stationed in Shanhaiguan is a part of the garrison permitted by the Boxer Protocol along the Beijing-Fengtian Railway. The force consists of two companies, approximately 230 infantry soldiers, plus wartime machine gun squads, communications teams, etc., seemingly possessing independent combat capabilities. Their barracks are located south of the railway, surrounded by permanent fortifications. The outer moat is several fathoms wide, and between the outer moat and the central fortress, there are multiple lines of trenches, totaling eight layers. The trenches are covered, preventing penetration by bullets and fragmentation from artillery shells. The communication trenches, traps, electric fences, etc., are all constructed using the latest post-World War methods. In the central location, there are also five cannons, sufficient to withstand attacks from the enemy for several days. Inside, there is a radio station capable of communicating with Japan. The facility is equipped to utilize solid fortifications to resist fiercely in case of attack, while simultaneously sending telegrams to request assistance, awaiting reinforcements. Since the withdrawal of our army from Jinzhou, the Japanese army stationed in Shanhaiguan has been preparing for action day and night. The garrison commander issued a note to He Zhuguo, commander of our Ninth Brigade, stating that if a single shot is fired within the area from Shanhaiguan to Qinhuangdao, a major incident would be unavoidable. Simultaneously, eleven Japanese warships arrived off the coast of Shanhaiguan. The fleet commander, Tsuda Shizue, also sent a note to Commander He, stating that the Japanese side would not prevent the withdrawal of the Chinese army from Jinzhou, but they would not be permitted to stop between Shanhaiguan and Qinhuangdao. If gunfire is detected within this area, the Japanese warships will take appropriate measures, etc. After receiving this note, Commander He knew that the Japanese army intended to provoke a conflict, so he ordered the troop trains to temporarily halt at Wantun (the first station outside Shanhaiguan). Commander He then dispatched locomotives to tow the trains through the pass at high speed, past Qinhuangdao, to Beidaihe, where they were transferred to other locomotives and sent to their destinations. When the troop trains passed through Yuguan, the Japanese army applauded and jeered on the platform. The general populace closed their doors and dared not watch. It took four days to transport all the Northeast Army into the pass. The Japanese army stationed in Yuguan, as the troop trains did not linger, had no opportunity to provoke a conflict, but it was still a close call. (January 6th)

Provocation by the Japanese Consul and Naval Captain in Fuzhou 81

▲Assassination Occurs Inside the Japanese Club

Fuzhou Correspondence: On the afternoon of January 2nd, the Anti-Japanese Associations of various schools in the provincial capital held an anti-Japanese art propaganda event at West Lake Park. Many people watched. The Japanese Consul, accompanied by the captain of the Kitakami, a warship anchored at the Mawei Naval Academy, also entered the park by car to watch. They actually tore down the posters on the wall and seized and tore up leaflets distributed by the students. Their attitude was extremely barbaric, causing a great uproar among the people. The Consul and Captain, realizing that the situation was unfavorable, hurriedly tried to flee the park. Unexpectedly, when they reached the bridge near the park entrance, the captain fell on the stone steps, injuring his forehead and bleeding slightly. He immediately drew his pistol and fired at the crowd. Fortunately, the soldiers and police maintaining order in the park arrived and stopped him, taking him to the city's Public Security Bureau, and in the evening, he was taken back to the consulate by car. The people were extremely indignant that the dignified Consul and Captain dared to provoke and commit violence in the park, and petitioned the provincial government, requesting that they telegraph the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a serious protest with the Japanese Ambassador. Unexpectedly, the next day, the Japanese Consul instead made three demands to the provincial government: punish the perpetrators, apologize, and ban the anti-Japanese movement. How this will be resolved in the future remains to be seen.

On the night of the 3rd, at 8:30 PM, in the Japanese club at Taigu Ping, Cangqian Mountain, the Japanese elementary school teacher, Mito San'yu, and his wife were suddenly assassinated. Mito was stabbed in the lower jaw, and his wife was stabbed in the neck. According to Mito's dying words, there were three murderers, but he did not mention their nationality before he died. It is investigated that the place is a gathering place for Japanese people, with tight security, and Chinese people rarely go there, let alone at night, it is even more difficult for Chinese people to enter the house. According to the investigation, the assassination was carried out by Taiwanese people who had a private feud with Mito. After receiving the report, the provincial government immediately sent Commissioner Chen Peikun to the consulate to inquire and to inspect the scene of the incident. On the morning of the 4th, the local court sent a prosecutor to examine the body, but was refused by the Japanese side. The funeral pyre was held that afternoon. The provincial government also convened an emergency meeting at 5 PM that afternoon, deciding that: 1) Regarding the assassination of Mito and his wife, regardless of the identity of the murderer, the provincial government should thoroughly investigate the matter. In addition to offering a reward of 10,000 yuan for the arrest of the murderer, the military and police are required to solve the case within 36 hours. 2) All anti-Japanese organizations from all walks of life will immediately cease operations. Elementary and middle schools in the provincial capital will start their winter vacation early from the 5th. 3) Martial law will be tightened. The 56th Division will dispatch a battalion, in coordination with the marine battalion originally stationed in Qiaonan, to guard the Cangqian Mountain and Fanchuanpu areas. Traffic will be stopped at 10 PM at night, and theaters will stop performing in the evening. Therefore, Fuzhou suddenly became tense again from the 5th.

Another dispatch: On the evening of the 3rd of this month, at 8:30 PM, in the dormitory of the Japanese elementary school attached to the Japanese club at Taigu Ping, Cangqian Mountain, the teacher Mito San'yu and his wife were assassinated. Mito was 30 years old, his wife 24, and they had been married for a year. Mito was stabbed in the lower jaw, and his wife suffered multiple injuries to the neck and lower abdomen. His wife died immediately, and Mito died on the way to the Fuzhou Boai Hospital. How the murderers came is still unclear. However, according to Japanese sources, Mito told someone before he died that three people broke into the house to commit the crime, one escaped from the front door and two from the back door, etc., but he did not mention why he was killed or the nationality of the murderers. That department is in Taigu Ping, where Chinese people rarely set foot, and even less so during the period of martial law. When asked, the doorman of the department did not know how the murderers came. There were also no differences on the door of the deceased's dormitory. Upon hearing the news, the provincial government immediately ordered the military and police agencies to strictly arrest the suspects, setting a deadline of 36 hours from 8 PM on the 4th to arrest the murderers, and offered a reward of 10,000 yuan in order to solve the case as soon as possible. Liu Shangzhi, the temporary martial law commander of Fuzhou, Li Dingzhang, the deputy commander, and Guo Yongyun, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, all expressed their resignation for the occurrence of this case, but it is unknown whether it will be approved. After this incident occurred, the Japanese warship Enoshima transported over a hundred sailors to Taijiang, who landed and went to the Japanese Consulate. More than fifty of them were stationed at the Dongying School and Fuxin Street Boai Hospital in Cangxia Zhou, and it was rumored that four Japanese warships were sailing from Sasebo to cause trouble under pretext. However, this case occurred in a remote place at night, and inside the house, which the military and police could not prevent. Our side does not bear any responsibility. (January 5th)

Riot of White Russians in Harbin 82

▲The Cause is the Heshengli Theft Case

▲More Than Ten Thousand People Gathered to Block Traffic

▲Injured Police and Seized Firearms

Harbin Correspondence: The White Russians residing in Harbin, their psychology of despising the Chinese people, has not diminished since the fall of the three northeastern provinces under the policy of non-resistance, since the demise of Imperial Russia. After the three Northeastern provinces fell, the White Russians saw the status of the Chinese people as even lower than slaves of a conquered nation. Incidents of assault and resistance to arrest have occurred in the city, and every time after being arrested, they impersonate Japanese citizens in hopes of being released by chance. The authorities are muddled and have no good way to deal with it, which further emboldens the White Russians. On the 2nd of this month, a major riot of White Russians occurred. The cause of this incident was that the Heshengli Cigarette, Wine, and Sundries Store, located at the corner of Central Street and Bread Street in Daoli District, was run by Li Yankui as the manager, with more than ten shop assistants. Their livelihood was not bad. On the 31st of last month, a White Russian named Jin Duoweichi, along with five men and women, went to the store, falsely claiming to be shopping and selecting items separately. After a long time, they rarely found anything that satisfied them. The manager Li Yankui found it quite strange, and carefully examined Jin Duoweichi's face, realizing that the man had come to shop many times, and every time after he left, the store would lose goods. Therefore, he paid attention to him. Sure enough, he saw the White Russian taking advantage of people's inattention to steal two Western shirts and a bag of candy, hiding them under his clothes. At the same time, one of the girls accompanying him also stole a box of sweets and stuffed it into her pocket. Li Yankui, having discovered the stolen goods, grabbed the two of them and refused to let go. The other Russians accompanying them actually beat Li viciously, injuring his head and face, and tearing his clothes. Jin Duoweichi even shouted that the Chinese were falsely accusing his daughter of stealing, and the Russians should rise up to defend her. As a result, many Russians passing by outside the door gathered, wanting to enter and join the beating. Just then, the nearby police arrived, pushed their way into the crowd, ordered the store to close the front door, and took the ringleader Jin Duoweichi away from the back door. After arriving at the police station, Jin Duoweichi presented a Lithuanian citizenship certificate, denying that he was a White Russian, and claiming that he had become a Japanese citizen, not acknowledging theft. As the case was minor, he was released. Unexpectedly, at around 5 PM on the afternoon of the 2nd of this month, a Russian woman, along with more than ten Russian thugs, came to Heshengli, claiming that Jin Duoweichi was her husband, and that he had been beaten and injured by the store for being falsely accused of theft, and had died in the hospital. They demanded that the store's personnel pay for his life. At that time, they directed the thugs to smash the goods in the store and dragged out the store manager Li Yankui, beating him severely on the spot. Li was seriously injured. Upon hearing the news, the Shangwu Street Police Station of the First Precinct urgently dispatched several police officers to mediate. The thugs resisted relying on their numbers. Subsequently, the First Precinct, upon hearing the news, dispatched a large team of police to disperse the crowd and rescue Li. By then, he was covered in injuries and barely breathing. He was immediately sent to the hospital for treatment. At this time, the police planned to arrest the leaders of the thugs. The thugs relied on their numbers and clamored, resisting arrest, and seizing the pistol of policeman Zhao Yongbin, pressing Zhao to the ground and beating him. Another thug climbed up and gave a speech, saying that it was the most shameful thing for a Russian to be beaten by the Chinese, the slaves of a conquered nation. The Chinese police should hand over the manager of Heshengli and send him to the Japanese consulate to be dealt with. At that time, many White Russians were listening, and they all agreed. Immediately, more than 10,000 people gathered. The road on Central Street, several miles long, was crowded with people, and traffic was blocked. Police officers on duty in various street sections could not perform their duties. Later, after the First Precinct dispatched more police officers to assist in maintaining traffic, they fired a row of shots into the air as a warning. However, the thugs not only did not disperse, but instead surrounded the police, and used wooden poles to raise the seized police hats, displaying them to the thoroughfare, mocking and laughing at each other. After 8 PM, the thugs dragged tables and chairs from the shops along the road to the center of the road, and piled them up across the street at the intersection of Bread Street and Central Street, blocking traffic. All vehicles, horses, and pedestrians were blocked. The street was originally a bustling street in Daoli District and a vital artery for the city's transportation, and at that time, it was completely blocked. Seeing that the situation was dangerous, the Heshengli store had already boarded up the doors and turned off the lights. At 8:30 PM, the thugs used axes and hammers to smash the store's signboard. At 8:40 PM, the Special Police Administration sent a fire truck to disperse the thugs with water hoses, but because there were too many people, it did not work and left. Later, the armed security team was also dispatched, but retreated due to the strength of the thugs. After 9 PM, the thugs' speeches became more intense. Some advocated immediately forming a volunteer army and asking the Japanese Consul to issue firearms. Some shouted that from today onwards, the Russians would occupy Central Street. Various strange slogans were endless. A member of the Japanese Consulate, at around 10 PM, passed through the blocked traffic in a car. White Russians rushed to clear the way, shouting "Long live the Japanese Empire." The Japanese Consulate member also deliberately showed the power of his imperialism, passing through the area four times. After 12 PM, there were no Chinese people on the streets. Russian thugs were still shouting in the thoroughfare, dismantling tables and chairs, holding wooden weapons, looking for Chinese people to beat. It was not until 4 AM on the 3rd, when the cold wind was piercing, that most of them could not stand it and gradually dispersed. Some thugs still used iron tools to smash Heshengli as they left. Because the doors and windows were made of iron, they were unable to do so, and then dispersed. On the way, they encountered police officers on duty, and chased after them, knocking out the police officers on duty in front of the China Bank branch and on 12th Street, and seizing their pistols. It was not until around 5 AM that it became quiet. (Morning of the 3rd) Continued letter on the 4th: Regarding the case of the Russian thugs gathering and rioting, yesterday, Wang Ruihua, the director of the Special Police Administration, went to see Zhang Jinghui late at night to ask for instructions. Zhang ordered that if the Russian thugs deliberately provoke trouble, they should maintain order within their authority. This morning (the 4th), Wang had ordered the security teams of various district offices to be on high alert. On the one hand, in order to appease the Russian thugs, the Heshengli grocery store where the incident occurred was sealed, and a notice was issued in Chinese and Russian, stating that they would send personnel to investigate the matter in order to handle the incident fairly. After the notice was issued, many Chinese and foreigners gathered to watch. In order to maintain order, the police dispatched a large team of armed police officers to patrol the streets to prevent the thugs from gathering again. Unexpectedly, at around 11 AM, the Russian thugs gradually gathered again in front of Heshengli. By 11:30 AM, there were already over a thousand people gathered. A thug said that the Chinese police authorities had already succumbed, but unless they took thorough measures, they would have to demand that the Heshengli personnel be handed over and sent to the Japanese Consulate for investigation. The crowd echoed him. At 12:10 PM, the thugs continued their work of blocking traffic by piling up tables, chairs, bricks, and stones in the center of the road. There were many vehicles, horses, and pedestrians coming and going that were intercepted at both ends. The police authorities could no longer tolerate this and dispatched two teams of armed security guards to set up checkpoints at the intersections of Central Street, first blocking pedestrians, and then sending personnel to persuade the thugs to remove the obstacles and disperse. The thugs did not listen and resisted with weapons. Therefore, the police fired several rows of shots, first firing into the air. The thugs stood still. Finally, they fired downward, injuring four people on the spot. The thugs then became fearful and wanted to escape. The police continued to fire, dispersing the thugs until they disappeared from Central Street. Only then did they stop shooting. Fearing that the thugs would gather again, they immediately set up posts along Central Street, prohibiting pedestrians and vehicles. From 12:40 PM in the afternoon until the morning of the 4th, the posts had not been removed. The security was strict at night. In addition to Central Street, the other streets were also filled with police officers on duty. Zhang Jinghui's temporary guard team was also dispatched to assist in patrolling and guarding throughout the night. The sound of gunfire was intermittent. At around 10 PM in the evening, the thugs gathered on Diagonal Street, intending to attack the police again. A Russian threw a hand grenade at the police, injuring a member of the guard team. They were dispersed by gunfire. That night, whenever three or four Russians gathered in any street, the police fired shots to disperse them. Fortunately, there were no incidents overnight. The shops on Central Street closed their doors and stopped business at noon on the 3rd when they heard the sound of gunfire. They gradually reopened this afternoon. When the Russian thugs were dispersed by the police, they carried their injured companions to the Japanese Consulate in Nangang to petition, demanding that the Japanese Consul protest to us, punish the police authorities, and arrest the Heshengli personnel. The Japanese Consul invited the representatives of the thugs inside and comforted them for a long time before the crowd dispersed. The situation in the city today is slightly calmer, but the police's precautions are still very tense. It is rumored that there is a Japanese background to this incident, as the Japanese side wants to advance into Harbin but is afraid of Soviet obstruction, so they incited the White Russians to create a pretext. Therefore, the authorities are not daring to slacken their precautions. Last night, Zhang Jinghui and the Special Police Administration issued the following notices: ▲Zhang Jinghui's Notice: Regarding the fact that the old Russian people residing in Harbin enjoy various treatments in China, which can be said to be unparalleled in the world. These expatriates should arouse their conscience and live and work in peace. However, on the 2nd and 3rd of this month, while celebrating the New Year, some unruly elements attempted to disrupt local security, using trivial trade matters as an excuse, gathering crowds, giving speeches arbitrarily in Central Street, blocking traffic, disrupting order, and disobeying police intervention, resulting in unfortunate incidents, which is greatly contrary to my consistent intention to protect expatriates. At this time of multiple incidents, I, as the governor, am busy day and night, constantly thinking about protecting expatriates and ensuring security, which should be well known to all parties. These expatriates, whether they have joined the nationality or not, should all share the difficulties of the times and be content with their duties. If there are any actions that endanger security, I, as the governor, for the sake of stabilizing the overall situation, can only enforce the law and will not be lenient in any way. In case of emergency, I will not hesitate to take the most severe measures, such as investigating their names, deporting them, and not allowing them to harm the public and delay the locality. As for the rights and wrongs of this incident, I will definitely investigate the details and handle it fairly, without any bias. This is a special notice.

▲Special Police Administration Notice: It has been investigated that on the evening of the 2nd of this month, a crowd of expatriates suddenly gathered and caused trouble in Daoli Central Street. Traffic was blocked for a time, the momentum was surging, and the atmosphere was tense. The office has briefly notified the public of the course and the actual situation of the settlement of the case. This matter arose from a lawsuit between the Chinese merchant Heshengli Candy Shop and expatriates Jin Duoweichi and others due to suspicion of theft. In fact, it was entirely caused by not understanding the true facts, which led to the spread of errors. The office has reported to the police

The report from the First Precinct states that on December 31st of last year, a patrol officer from the Shangwu Street Police Station reported that at 6 PM on the same day, Li Yankui, the manager of Heshengli Candy Shop, located at the corner of Central Street and Bread Street, reported that several Russians were shopping in the store, taking the opportunity to steal things, etc. They went to arrest one person, and found Shigeleta candies in his pocket, which the merchant identified as stolen goods. They were sent to the precinct, where the plaintiff Li Yankui was questioned, who provided the same information. How was the truth? How was it right and wrong? Without detailed investigation, it was impossible to determine. Unexpectedly, on the evening of January 2nd, a crowd gathered because of this case, and there were various rumors, which were all beyond the facts and reason. The presentation for consideration and verification came forward, the office detailed the truth of the case, but that's it. The handling was not very wrong, but at this time, the outside world did not understand the truth, and false statements were rampant, and even used words to frighten the public, and there were even reports that expatriate Jin Duoweichi had died in the hospital. It happened that it was the New Year's holiday, and many expatriates were walking on the streets. Among them, a small number of floating elements, without examining the truth and falsehood, listened to the one-sided propaganda, causing the storm to rise sharply, and a chorus of hundreds of people gathered to cause trouble in the street. They arbitrarily shouted in the street, disobeyed the resolution, and first demanded that the small shop remove the plaque and close the business, and then hindered order, traffic, and even beat up and snatched the police's firearms, and hindered municipal fire trucks from being able to rescue the fire, until midnight before they dispersed. The office has been supervising the police to protect the security achievements for months, as well as the fact that there are military police standing upright, and the strength is sufficient, as everyone knows. For this kind of thing, how can we not forcibly stop it, just to deeply understand that the addition of a temporary addition is blind following, and most of them are expatriate masses without nationality, and usually rely on our police for protection, so we trace the original heart, firmly instruct all officials and police to exercise restraint and self-respect, and are unwilling to rush to apply pressure, only in the distant parts around, arrange prevention, and wait for self-enlightenment, this is the hard work of the office to deal with at that time, which should be understood by all the expatriate masses. Now the office still upholds the spirit of peace and generosity, in addition to investigating whether there are any unscrupulous elements who have other purposes and hope to incite incidents, we will handle them separately, and will not deeply investigate the ignorant youth and expatriate masses. After seeing this notice, the expatriate masses should also live and work in peace, and must not listen to rumors again and bring guilt upon themselves. Regarding the case of the Heshengli small shop and Jin Duoweichi, whether it is theft or false accusation, after a clear investigation, listen to the court's fair decision, and the small shop has temporarily suspended business as the cause of the incident. Jin Duoweichi is safe and sound, and the story of being beaten to death is even more self-defeating. As for the officials and police in charge of this case in the relevant police station, if there are any omissions and dereliction of duty after the investigation, the office will also punish and warn them equally, and will never protect them. In addition to supervising and urging them to handle them separately, it is urgently combined to notify the public.

Bandit Forces in Huangpi Gradually Subdued 83

▲Bandits Building Fortifications in Changxuanling

Hankou Correspondence: The Red Bandits of Huangpi, after being jointly suppressed by the Fourth Division of Xu Tingyao, the Thirteenth Division of Xia Douyin, the Thirtieth Division of Li Mingzhong, and the Forty-fourth Division of Xiao Zhichu, have now retreated to Changxuanling, Yanzigang, Tieshidun, and other places. There are no bandit traces near the county seat, and the Pinghan Railway has suffered no losses. It is investigated that Kuang's bandit plan originally intended to seize the Huangpi County seat, destroy the railway, and then take Wuhan. Later, they abandoned the plan to attack the city and detoured south in order to disperse our army's strength and then attempt to defeat them one by one. However, due to the strong force of the government troops, they could not succeed. The number of bandits killed in battle has reached two or three out of ten. At the same time, there was a lack of unified command within the bandits, and the bandit soldiers were mostly coerced and lacked fighting spirit. In order to preserve their strength, Kuang concentrated most of his forces in Changxuanling and other places to build fortifications, hoping to hold on. The remaining small forces are scattered in Wangjiahe, Xujiaqiao, Fengjiaqiao, Hengshan, Changyan, Luohansi, Xinglongji, and other places. About one regiment is stationed in Changyan, and the rest are stationed with a thousand or several hundred. The bandits are not afraid of the pressure of the government troops, but they dare not love war due to internal discord. The government troops have now taken the initiative to make contact and pursue forward. Xu Tingyao, the commander of the Fourth Division, who was supervising the suppression in Hengdian, returned to Hankou on the 8th and met with He Chengjun on the 9th to report everything. It is heard that it is planned to defeat the main force of the bandits before the 15th and then find a way to wipe out the remaining bandits. However, the bandit's den in Changxuanling has strong fortifications, and there are mortars, machine guns, and various combat weapons. When a large-scale attack is launched, there may still be fierce battles. (January 9th)

Shanxi Provincial Currency Plunges 85

▲ Slow issuance of financial bonds is the main reason

▲ Tight credit and rising prices in the market

Taiyuan Communication: The provincial government previously obtained approval from the national government and the Legislative Yuan for the issuance of Shanxi Province Financial Reorganization Bonds. Therefore, it originally intended to withdraw the provincial currency, believing it had an eleven-percent grasp of the situation. Thus, in November of last year, it officially announced that starting from the 15th of this year, the provincial currency would be redeemed at a rate of 1 jiao 5 fen per yuan. At the same time, it strictly ordered merchants and others to use the banknotes at a rate of 1 jiao 5 fen in silver before the actual redemption. However, since the promulgation of the announcement, general silver houses and various merchants have held a skeptical attitude. The silver houses even negotiated to temporarily suspend business in an invisible way, expressing opposition to the use of provincial currency at 1 jiao 5 fen. Although ordinary merchants did not dare to openly object on the surface, the prices of goods soared. Because of this, the value of the currency plummeted, and credit became tighter. As of recently, with only half a month left before the redemption date, the central government has not yet approved the issuance of the financial bonds that the provincial government hoped for. The general public is once again taking a wait-and-see attitude regarding the redemption on January 15th, and the value of the currency has plummeted, becoming increasingly severe. In the black market, it is not easy to buy one yuan of silver with eleven or twelve yuan of provincial currency. The provincial government authorities, seeing this situation, are deeply worried. Yesterday, they announced to the public the difficulty of redeeming on schedule on January 15th, in order to dispel public doubts. The full text of the announcement is recorded below to show a glimpse of the financial future of Shanxi Province: [Since the price of provincial currency has declined,

the financial situation in the market has been extremely chaotic, and merchants and the public alike feel difficulties, and tax revenues have also been affected. If relief is not sought early, not only will all industries wither, but also government administration will be difficult to carry out. However, the face value of the currency is huge, and the treasury has few funds. To completely withdraw it, we rely on the recovery of financial bonds. Therefore, since its reorganization, the provincial government has repeatedly telegraphed the central government and sent representatives to make urgent requests. Fortunately, considering the hardships, it agreed to restore the last ten days of last month. Received a telegram from Ma, a member of the provincial government, stating that the bond regulations have been reviewed and passed by the Legislative Yuan and stipulate that they will be issued on January 1, 1932. The provincial government deeply believes that from now on, the province’s finances can be reorganized with this, and the suffering of merchants and the public can be relieved with this. Therefore, resolutely decided at the 15th temporary meeting of the provincial government on the 20th of last month to pre-announce the withdrawal measures to comfort the public. Unexpectedly, the national government has not yet announced it after many days. The provincial government, feeling the urgency of the situation, could not wait any longer. It again telegraphed the Executive Yuan to quickly submit it to the national government for announcement and telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to print the banknotes for issuance at that time. Recently, received a telegram from the Executive Yuan, stating that it has been forwarded to the national government for verification, etc. Later, received an urgent telegram from Ma, stating that the central government is busy preparing for the First Plenary Session of the Central Committee, and the Ministry of Finance is rushing to hand over matters, and no one is proposing the announcement of the regulations, and the banknotes cannot be printed based on them, etc. The withdrawal of provincial currency in this province was originally based on government bonds as the only source of funds. Now that the government bonds have not been received as scheduled, the previous proposal to exchange government bonds with provincial currency at 40% on January 1, 1932, cannot be implemented. At the same time, the funds designated for borrowing with government bonds cannot be established. The method of exchanging each yuan of provincial currency for 1 jiao 5 fen in silver on January 15 is also difficult to achieve as scheduled. Although the provincial government is deeply worried, the government bonds are delayed due to some reason, and the matter has changed suddenly, and there is nothing that can be done. However, the provincial government’s determination to withdraw the provincial currency will never be relaxed because of this. In addition to urging the central government to announce it as soon as possible, we are still raising cash. Once the government bonds are received, we will set another date and still handle it according to the original proposal, and we will never change our original intention due to the central government’s delay, causing panic among the merchants and the public of the entire Shanxi Province. For this reason, this announcement is made, and all merchants and the public are informed, and do not generate doubts and cause disturbances, which is most important.] (January 2nd)

Liu Guitang Requests No Troops Be Sent to Monitor 86

Jinan Communication: Liu Guitang, Guo Mafeng and their troops gathered at Dakou and boarded trains to Gaotang in northern Shandong for reorganization. Han Fuju, for the sake of prudence, specifically ordered the Beiping armored train and troops along the route to be prepared. Last night, Gu Liangmin, commander of the 22nd Division stationed in Yanzhou, and Liu Shuxiang, director of the staff office of the headquarters, telegraphed Han to report that Liu Guitang had sent Xia Ziming as a representative to Yanzhou. According to Xia, Liu, Guo and their troops were eager to surrender and had already marched from Dabianqiao to Dakou on foot on the 7th. However, they were uneasy about the news of the armored train and troops along the route monitoring them and requested: 1) Do not send armored trains and troops to monitor them; 2) After gathering at Dakou, immediately conduct the reorganization so that they can search for the remaining bandits in the mountains nearby. After the reorganization, they are willing to go to Gaotang on foot and do not want to take the train; 3) At the beginning of the pacification, they should be treated with leniency to show magnanimity and avoid complications. Liu, Guo and their troops made this request because they were aware of the three incidents that occurred during Zhang Zongchang’s time, when they boarded trains at Dakou during reorganization. After receiving the telegram, Han telegraphed Liu’s representative Xia Ziming to come to Ji today (the 8th) for consultation and decision. The outgoing and incoming telegrams are recorded below: (Gu

Liangmin’s telegram) Limited to immediate arrival, addressed to Commander Han Jun, Zimi: 1) The Yuwucan telegram has been received. Liu Guitang’s representative Xia Ziming came to Yan and stated that the troops are very sincere about surrendering, and Yu has already departed from Bianqiao. If armored trains and troops are sent to monitor them, I am afraid that misunderstandings will occur, which would be unfortunate. Please do not send armored trains and troops to show good faith. Please telegraph instructions on whether this is acceptable. 2) According to Xia Ziming, Liu, Guo and others want to be reorganized at Dakou in order to recruit the remaining bandits from Nanshan. When they depart in the future, they are willing to go on foot and do not want to take the train. 3) At the beginning of the incorporation, they should be treated with leniency to show magnanimity. If there are too many restrictions, complications may arise. Please make a decision. Yours respectfully, Gu Liangmin Liu Xunxiang, Yu Shen. (Han Fuju’s reply) Limited to immediate arrival, addressed to Yanzhou Division Commander Gu Jingxuan, Director Liu Weizhen: The Yu Shen telegram reporting the requests of the representatives of Liu, Guo and their troops has been received. Please have Xia Ziming come to Ji quickly for detailed discussion and decision. This is the reply. Han Fuju, Qi Shen Yin Can.

Qingdao Party Affairs in Dispute 87

▲ Lower-level party departments oppose the municipal party department

▲ Declare secession and form a separate office

Qingdao Communication: Disputes have also arisen in Qingdao’s party affairs. Yesterday, the executive and supervisory committee members of various districts and branches held a joint meeting and resolved that, starting from the 7th, all lower-level party departments and all party members would sever ties with the current municipal party department. On the one hand, they telegraphed the central government to report the misdeeds of the members of the municipal party department and requested a thorough reorganization. On the other hand, they established a joint office of the district party departments to temporarily carry out the city’s party affairs. They also issued a declaration, publicizing the misdeeds of the executive and supervisory committee members, listing a total of ten items. At the same time, the municipal party department also issued a letter to all party members in the city today, advising all party members to prioritize the country’s interests when the country is facing difficulties and not to be provoked by others, giving others an opportunity to take advantage of. It is divided into four key points: 1) Party comrades should unite sincerely and overcome national difficulties together; 2) This association is happy to accept any suggestions from comrades in the city. Within the scope of possibility, we are willing to work with comrades in the city to plan and proceed to perfect party affairs day by day. 3) When foreign insults are imminent, we should strictly abide by order and make arduous struggles; otherwise, we are creating opportunities for imperialists, which is like inviting thieves into the house, and although we love the country on the surface, we are actually harming the country. 4) The country is on the verge of peril. All comrades should take the national interest as the prerequisite and should not be nitpicking and alienating the people, speaking for the imperialists. Finally, it is said that party comrades should strive in time and engage in disciplined national salvation undertakings, and not allow the slightest retreat to foreign enemies, and be sincere to comrades in the party, etc. It is not yet certain whether the lower-level party departments will end their activities due to this advice. (January 7th)

Local Communications

Songjiang 88

Rampant Piracy at the Junction of Songjiang and Fengxian. A large number of bandits, estimated to be over a thousand, have recently been discovered outside the Tuolin seawall at the junction of Songjiang and Fengxian. It is rumored that they are the former subordinates of Taibao A-shu, who fled into the sea. All areas west from Caojing and east to Tuolin are occupied by these bandits, leading to frequent robberies. The law-abiding citizens have all fled. It is now rumored that the heads of the fifteenth district of Songjiang have jointly petitioned the Songjiang County Government to dispatch troops for strict suppression. Fengxian is also preparing to clear the area.

Nantong 89

Chamber of Commerce Maintains Finance in the City. Nantong’s money houses have been affected by the disaster and the current situation, making it impossible to recover loans. Silver businesses from Shanghai and other ports have come to squeeze money, causing panic in the market. On the 9th, the county chamber of commerce sent Sheng Bo and others to Shanghai to contact various banks and money houses to provide as much relief as possible to Nantong’s money industry. At the same time, it notified all industries to contact local money houses before the end of the accounting period, settle accounts, and continue business, so that the market can circulate.

Lusi Pirates Rampant. In the area of ​​Lusi Sanjia Town, a large number of pirates have recently arrived, demanding ransoms and looting fishing boats, causing great disturbances. Fishermen have appealed to the province. The Department of Industry is convening a meeting to protect fishermen to discuss relief measures.

Boundary Disputes Between Tonghai Counties Unresolved. Recently, there has been a lot of disputes between Nantong and Haimen counties over the boundaries of the Minzaosha area. Although the provincial committee has conducted two on-site inspections, it has not been resolved. The county government is submitting the case to the province for a final decision.

Xiaoshan 90

Frequent Robberies in Four Villages. There have been many robberies in the four villages of Xiaoshan recently. On the 3rd night, the homes of Chen Shouqing and Chen Zuwang, merchants in Tangli outside the East Gate, were robbed, with losses exceeding a thousand gold. On the 7th night, the homes of four farmers, Du Aliang, Du Guoxiang, Du Changxian, and Du Juxian in Dujiatang, Qiujiang Township, were robbed by more than ten bandits armed with torches, with losses also exceeding a thousand gold. Du Aliang’s family suffered the greatest losses. They have jointly reported to the county government requesting investigation and arrest.

Fengxian 91

Kidnapping Case Cracked in Fengxian. The 6th District Xulibao Security Group has recently received reports that there are kidnapped victims hidden in Bizheng Township, about three li from the town. Last night (the 8th) at 12 o’clock, they led the entire team to rush to the back of a Lu family farmhouse in that area and found a male child victim. Two bandits who were watching the victim, Lu Xingsheng and Yuan Lushi, were also arrested on the spot and taken back to the team for questioning overnight. According to Lu, the child was kidnapped from Ganpu Town, Haiyan, Zhejiang, and was sent by a friend from Shanghai on December 26 of last year to be raised. Yuan Lushi said that Xingsheng was her nephew. The day before yesterday, he said that someone was raising a child and gave her two yuan as wages, so she dared to take him in, and she didn't know anything else. The child was further interrogated and could speak. He claimed to be surnamed Chen, named Guan, five years old, living in Dongjie, Ganpu, Haiyan. His father was a businessman in Shanghai. This time, because of the major robbery in Putown, he was taken out by Lu Xingsheng, laid on the boat for many days until he arrived in the countryside a few days ago and was looked after by the old woman (referring to Yuan Lushi), and was not allowed to come out, etc. However, he claimed not to know the name of his parents. According to the confession of the district office, in addition to sending the two bandits to the county for interrogation today, they also asked the county to send the police to go to the county to find out where they are, so that they can be claimed.

Changshu 92

Conflict Between Police Team and Security Group. The Xigang Town District Office in Nansha District of this county originally had a security group to maintain local security. On the morning of the 9th, five or six members of the group went to Donglai Town to meet the group leader. However, the members who went were all in plain clothes, and they were wearing box cannons. After arriving in Donglai Town, the group leader was not found. One of the members suddenly played with the box cannon for some reason and fired three shots with live ammunition. Yang, the sergeant of the town police team, heard about it and immediately led the police to investigate. They saw many people in plain clothes holding box cannons and went forward to question them. They replied that they were security members here to meet the group leader. When they checked their badges, they found that they were not carrying them. Because the police team suspected them, they confiscated their guns and arrested the five people in plain clothes at the police team headquarters. The Xigang Security Group also sent a telegram to testify, but because the badges were incomplete, they could not be tolerated during this winter defense period. It is decided that the five arrested persons will be sent to the general team headquarters in the city on the 10th to await disposal.

Dispute Between Village Teachers and Pond School Over School Buildings. The school buildings of the rural normal school in Pucheng District of this county were originally connected to Tangqiao Elementary School. Before the rural normal school was opened, Tangqiao Elementary School borrowed many rooms. Later, after the Education Bureau built a new school building for Tangqiao Elementary School, the rural normal school planned to take back the old school building. However, Xu Peineng, the principal of Tangqiao Elementary School, refused to hand it over. The Education Bureau had ordered them to hand it over three times without any effect. The other day, Xiao Li, the principal of the rural normal school, notified the school on the one hand, and on the other hand, moved out the desks of Tangqiao Elementary School. As a result, students' books and stationery were scattered and lost. Therefore, the elementary school students went to question Xiao Li, the principal of the rural normal school, in teams. It is not known why a violent conflict occurred, resulting in the serious injury of three students from Tangqiao Elementary School. They immediately went to the city to ask the county for an examination of the injuries. The school immediately went on strike and formed a team to march, give speeches, distribute leaflets, paste slogans, and shout slogans such as "Down with Xiao Li, the principal of the rural normal school." The Education Bureau heard the report and sent Xu Zhirui, the head of the social education section, to the countryside on the 8th to investigate. As of the afternoon of the 9th, Tangqiao Elementary School had not resumed classes. However, according to news from the rural normal school, it was said that there was no such thing as beating students from Tangqiao Elementary School. Only that on the afternoon of the 7th, when the students from Tangqiao Elementary School rushed into the rural normal school, many students fell to the ground, and there were photos to prove it. The three injured students from Tangqiao Elementary School have been examined and confirmed by the county that they have injuries. In the future, the principals of the two schools will inevitably confront each other in court.

Hefei 93

Kidnapping occurred outside the Water West Gate. Since winter, robberies have occurred one after another in the four villages around here, but they are all in places a little far from the city. Suddenly, last night at about 8 o'clock, more than 20 bandits broke into the Lujiahuayuan Village near the Shuixi Gate, robbing more than a dozen households along the door without any exception. Before leaving, they kidnapped a young girl surnamed Lü who was 18 years old and took away six oxen. When the commander of the Shuixi Gate heavy battalion Hu Bichen heard the alarm, he urgently sent troops to pursue and arrest them, but they had already disappeared.

Hangzhou 94

Large quantity of red pills seized in Xincheng Market. Last night at about 8 o'clock, a boatman from Zhakou, Shan Hongde, was carrying ten iron boxes containing a large number of red pills, a total of 100,000 pills, through Yanling Road in Hangzhou Xincheng Market. His expression was flustered, and Wu Hong, a patrol officer from the Second District Police Station, saw that his behavior was suspicious, and led the police to check and found them on the spot. He was immediately taken into custody and questioned by Liu Qing, a staff member. He confessed that he was entrusted by a customer to load them from Kaihua Huabu to Hangzhou. Because the case involves criminal matters, a document was sent to the Public Security Bureau to transfer them to the court for interrogation.

Huzhou 95

Traitor Zhou Haishan executed by shooting. The Seventh Regiment Headquarters of the Huzhou Security Team recently learned that Zhou Haishan, the former head of the Changxing Dashiqiao Security Group, was involved in treason. Regiment Commander Shen ordered the Third Company of the Security Team stationed in Lijia Lane, Changxing, to arrest him and escort him to Huzhou. The regiment headquarters interrogated him, and Zhou Haishan directly confessed to treason. The provincial government approved the death penalty. Yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, a team was sent to escort the Zhou Haishan criminal to the Zhongjia Lane entrance near Lüshan and executed him by shooting.

Jiangyin 96

Fushi girl commits suicide by drowning. The Fushi Girls' Middle School outside the East Gate was founded by an American Christian. It has more than 280 female students. The other day (

8th), a female student named Dong Huamei suddenly committed suicide by drowning in the Zhongshan Gate in the early morning. The reason is unknown. Dong is a Suzhou native, 17 years old. Because her father gambled and bankrupted the family, her mother worked as a helper outside and sold her daughter to a brothel. Later, Gu Shigang, a Shanghai native, saw her pitiful background and redeemed her to study at Fushi. After she had committed suicide in the sixth grade, the school principal, Wang Shengshan, took her back after being examined by the Public Security Bureau and telegraphed Gu Shigang in Shanghai to come to Cheng to handle the matter.

Gaoyou 97

Large number of kidnapped victims ransomed. More than ten bandits suddenly came to Nangantu, the ninth district of this county, and robbed the villagers. They then kidnapped seven people, including Zhou Wenliang, Zhou Wenqi, Yi Changgeng, Yang Hengxing's grandson, Yang Jizhong's wife, and Yang Guangxing's two daughters. Now, Yang and other kidnapped victims have all been ransomed. However, although Yi Changgeng's family negotiated with the bandits with a large sum of money, there is still no news of him. Yi's father, Jiu Yu, has come to the city to ask the county government to arrest Chen Fuqing, who has been in contact with the bandits, and investigate the whereabouts of his son.

Wuxi 98

Water Pumping Machinery Users Oppose the Collection of Donations. The district heads of this county requested the county government and the provincial department to collect donations for water pumping machinery licenses due to insufficient funds. The Water Pumping Association opposed it, and the provincial government rejected it at the 410th meeting. Recently, the district heads have repeatedly used the threat of resignation to fight for the rights of the water pumping machinery users. More than 500 people, including Yang Yuru, heard the news and were furious. Yesterday, they continued to submit a petition to the provincial department to request that the collection be stopped to avoid causing suffering to the people.

The Third District Fire Brigade Established. The merchants and people of Nanqiao Town, the third district (Yangming Township) of this county, initiated the organization of a fire brigade and reported it to the Fire Brigade Federation for record. It was named the Wuxi 36th Section Fire Brigade and held its founding ceremony yesterday afternoon. The fire brigades from various sections of the city sent representatives to the countryside to participate, which was quite a grand occasion for a time.

Ningbo 99

Five Elementary School Students Enlist in the Army. Five students from the first and second grades of the private Feidi Junior Elementary School in Ningbo, Huang Meiding, Chen Desheng, Zhou Mingqi, Zhu Zhengrui, and Li Linzhen, suddenly had the idea of ​​enlisting in the army after seeing news reports of Jinzhou's fall and the Japanese army attacking Shanhaiguan. They explained their aspirations to the school authorities and wanted to leave the school to join the army. The school authorities did not grant their request because the students Huang Meiding and others were too young (the ages of the five students were all under 15 years old). The students were very angry because they did not get permission from the school authorities and secretly ran away together on the morning of the 7th to join the army.

Zhenjiang 100

Representatives of Fishermen's Associations from Various Counties Petition. This morning, the representatives of fishermen's associations from various counties in Jiangsu Province went to the provincial government and the departments of civil affairs, finance, and industry with petitions. The petitions included two points: 1) Fishermen often have salt used by salt police in various places colluding with unscrupulous fishers to extort money from the fishermen. Please ask the provincial government to consult the Ministry of Finance to strictly prohibit it and issue a prohibition. 2) The water police in various places cannot protect the fishermen and are sometimes harmed by them. The fishermen's self-defense groups are difficult to unify under the administration of the county government and have various difficulties. It is proposed to abolish or reduce the scope of the four district water police and reorganize all military equipment into fishery police. If the government's funds are insufficient, the local government will raise them on its own. The provincial government was represented by Section Chief He, who agreed to convey the message to Chairman Gu. Director Zhao of the Department of Civil Affairs personally came out to meet them and expressed acceptance and consideration. The representatives were satisfied and left.

Sun, Wu, Kong, and Yang to Travel to Ningbo by Steamer Today 101

▲Proceeding to Xikou to Meet Chiang Kai-shek

▲Zhang Jingjiang and Others Will Also Go to Meet Him

▲National Crisis Demands His Swift Return

▲Sun Cables Hong Kong and Guangzhou, Urging Hu to Come to the Capital

Sun Ke, the President of the Executive Yuan, had originally planned to travel to Hangzhou yesterday morning by car, and then proceed to Fenghua to personally meet Chiang Kai-shek and urge him to come to the capital to jointly salvage the critical situation. However, because traveling to Hangzhou would involve a roundabout route, causing too many transfers and wasting time, it was decided after discussion that they would instead take the Ning-Shao Company's new Ning-Shao steamer at 5:00 PM today, heading directly to Ningbo. Those traveling with Sun to Xikou by long-distance bus are Wu Tiecheng, Kong Xiangxi, Yang Shuzhuang, a party of four, and their staff.

Upon returning to Shanghai on the 13th, Sun Ke, Wu Tiecheng, Kong Xiangxi, Yang Shuzhuang, and their party decided on their travel date yesterday. Yesterday morning, they telegraphed Fenghua to notify Chiang. Simultaneously, the municipal government telegraphed Wang Shihe, Chiang's adjutant, requesting him to send someone to meet them at the dock and prepare long-distance buses to go directly to Xikou. They are scheduled to arrive in Ningbo at 6:00 AM on the 12th and expect to meet with Chiang around 8:00 AM. According to Wu Tiecheng's statement to our newspaper reporter, they hope to return to Shanghai on the 13th after meeting with Chiang.

▲Zhang Ji and Others to Follow. Our newspaper reporter interviewed Wu Tiecheng yesterday, who said that the national situation is now critical, and the people of the country unanimously hope that Hu, Wang, and Chiang will jointly come forward to maintain the overall situation. Mr. Chiang had previously stated that his personal advancement or retreat would depend on the will of the people of the country. Therefore, at this critical moment, Mr. Chiang will surely respond to the unanimous demand of the people and come to the capital. We four will first take a steamer to Ningbo tomorrow (i.e., today) and return after meeting with Chiang. Mr. Zhang Ji, Zhang Jingjiang, Ye Chucang, and others will continue to go to Fenghua to urge his swift return. It is expected that they will be able to set off in two or three days.

Yu Youren Not Coming Yet. Yu Youren, the President of the Control Yuan, did not come to Shanghai yesterday morning. The central government has already appointed Yu as a representative to go to Hong Kong to urge Hu Hanmin to come to the capital. Yu is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai from the capital this morning and take a steamer to Hong Kong on the 13th.

Chen Youren Arrives in Shanghai. Foreign Minister Chen Youren arrived in Shanghai from the capital by car at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. He is staying at Sun Ke's residence on Moliai Road and is scheduled to return to the capital today.

Sun Visits Huang Hanliang. Around 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, Sun Ke drove to visit Finance Minister Huang Hanliang to discuss ways to maintain financial stability. The discussion lasted a long time before they concluded.

▲Sun Cables Hu Hanmin. After deciding on the date to go to Fenghua yesterday, Sun cabled Hu Hanmin to inform him and urged him with the most sincere words to overcome his illness and go north. At the same time, he also cabled Tang Shaochuan and others in Guangzhou, asking them to urge Hu nearby. The original texts of the two telegrams are recorded below. To Mr. Hu Zhantang, 8 Miaogao Terrace, Hong Kong: The national crisis has reached a point where it is truly the last test of whether our party can take on the responsibility of saving the country. I have been in the capital for two weeks, but the central government is empty, and without guidance, major plans for foreign affairs and domestic administration cannot be carried out. The previous declaration to the people of the whole country that we would unite as a party to save the country is now impossible to answer the people. After repeated consideration, I can only make the most sincere request to you, Mr. Wang, and Mr. Chiang. Mr. Wang has indicated that his illness has slightly subsided and he will do his best to come to the capital. Comrades in the capital have decided to ask Mr. Yu Youren to represent them in going to Hong Kong to urge your return. I am also scheduled to go to Fenghua tomorrow to urge Mr. Chiang. I hope that you, for the sake of the party and the country, will put aside everything and come to the capital immediately. This is not only my personal plea, but also the unanimous appeal of the people of the whole country and all comrades in the party. Sun Ke bows (10th).

Telegraph to Tang Shaochuan and Others. To Mr. Tang Shaochuan, Mr. Deng Zhiru, Mr. Xiao Focheng, Mr. Chen Bonan, Mr. Liu Jiwen in Guangzhou, and convey to all comrades, and to Mr. Wu Tiyun, Mr. Chen Choushuo, Mr. Zhang Huichang in Hong Kong: The greatest goal of the plenary session of the First National Congress is to unite our party and resolve the national crisis. This is truly the unanimous demand of the whole country and the whole party today. However, since the fall of Jinzhou, the people of the country have been calling out, but Mr. Hu, Wang, and Chiang have not been able to resolutely come to the capital. Therefore, the central government is empty and everything is stagnant. A person without any real power is forced to bear the responsibility of the central administration, which is exhausting and does not help the country. After repeated consideration, I can only make the most sincere request to Mr. Hu, Wang, and Chiang to save this dying party and country. Mr. Wang has indicated that his illness has slightly improved and he will come to the capital even if he has to be supported by his illness, so there should be no problem. I have decided to go to Fenghua tomorrow to urge Mr. Chiang to come to the capital immediately. At the same time, comrades in the capital have entrusted Mr. Yu Youren to go to Hong Kong to urge Mr. Hu to overcome his illness and take up his post to jointly shoulder the great responsibility. We must do our best to carry out this movement of uniting to save the country. For me personally, what I do for the party and the country lies in this one move. If I still do not get the approval of the three gentlemen, I can only resign and dare not prolong this situation, which would delay the party and the country. I also urge all comrades to unanimously advocate and urge Mr. Hu to come north immediately. I await and pray. Sun Ke bows (10th).

Yesterday, University Students Held a Memorial Service for Yang Tongheng 102

▲Thousands of Students Participated

▲Parade with the Coffin in the British and French Concessions

▲Police Intervention Caused Minor Disturbances

The Shanghai University Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation held a memorial service for Yang Tongheng, a student who died during a petition in Nanjing, at the Public Sports Field in Nanshi at 10:00 AM yesterday. Several thousands of people from all walks of life participated. The atmosphere at the venue was quite solemn. Students who went to Nanjing reported on the martyr's death. The details are recorded as follows:

Participating Organizations. Most of the participants yesterday were from the student community. Many representatives from major middle schools and universities attended, including students from Jinan University, Guanghua University, Fudan University, School of Law and Political Science, Jiaotong University, Xinhua Art College, Guanghua Middle School Attached, Fudan Middle School Attached, Datong Middle School Attached, and other schools, as well as the Chinese People's Foreign Affairs Support Association, various labor unions, totaling about two thousand people.

Coffin at the Venue (Photo by Wang Kai)

▲Venue Arrangement. The venue was at the Public Sports Field, with an altar in the center, a portrait of martyr Yang Tongheng hanging above, and many elegiac couplets hanging on the sides. There were also wreaths sent by various students, placed on both sides. The weather was cloudy and gloomy, and the north wind was piercingly cold. Flags flew in the air, creating a very sad atmosphere.

▲Proceedings. The meeting began at 10:45 AM. Initially, student Wen Sheng reported on Yang's death in Nanjing, the details of which were reported in the newspapers at the time. In addition to female students, many women participated in the audience, many of whom wept incessantly. After the report, everyone bowed three times to the portrait, and the chairman presented a wreath.

▲Parade in the Concessions. After the meeting, the crowd carried Yang's coffin and paraded. They departed from the Public Sports Field, crossed Fangxie Road and entered Zhonghua Road, turned to Minguo Road, exited the Xiaobeimen, reached the Great World on Xizang Road, arrived at Nanjing Road, turned east to Sizhong Road, and then went north to Sichuan Road Bridge and Tianqiao Road. At this point, they were dispersed by Chinese and Western detectives from the Public Concession police.

Police Surveillance. During the parade, the British and French concessions, fearing that the students marching in formation would cause trouble, sent detectives to monitor. At the borders of the Chinese, French, and British concessions, temporary martial law was implemented, and the small iron gates at the borders were tightly closed, cutting off traffic and creating a very serious situation.

Disturbances. There were over a thousand people in the parade. When they reached the Public Concession, the Central Police Station sent Chinese and Western detectives to monitor them. The detectives were armed with guns and ammunition, and red armored vehicles carrying armed police officers slowly followed behind. When they reached Broadway Road, because the area was very narrow, the large number of people in the parade caused a sudden interruption of traffic. The police then dispersed them, and the crowd had no choice but to disperse. It was reported that one student was arrested at 1:00 PM.

Yang's Coffin Placed. After the parade, the coffin of martyr Yang Tongheng was carried by the crowd, but was blocked on Broadway Road. It was then moved to the Sichuan Businessmen's Association on Jiangwan Road in Zhabei. Because Yang was from Sichuan, his family members are coming to Shanghai as soon as possible and plan to transport his body back to his hometown.

French Concession Closes Iron Gates at the Sino-French Border (Photo by this Newspaper)

Feng Yuxiang Gave a Speech at the YMCA Yesterday 104

▲Christian Youth Should Have Revolutionary Spirit

According to Zhonghua News Agency, Mr. Feng Huanzhang was invited to give a speech at the Zhongshan Hall on the fifth floor of the National YMCA of China on Museum Road in Shanghai yesterday (10th) at 3:00 PM. The audience was extremely crowded. After the chairman introduced him, Mr. Feng Huanzhang began his speech, briefly stating, "During this time of national crisis, our only responsibility is how to overcome this national crisis and how to prevent the words 'slave of a fallen nation' from being placed on our heads. We can only demonstrate the spirit of Christian youth from the time of the founding of the Republic to turn the tide." In the past, most revolutionaries were Christian youth who desperately worked forward, with a spirit of perseverance. If they failed, they would hide in the YMCA and do work. When there was an opportunity, they would go to the people to do revolutionary work. We Christian youth now need that kind of spirit to overcome this national crisis. Now society has become a society where dragons beget dragons, phoenixes beget phoenixes, and mice raise children who know how to burrow. To be honest, it has become a state where the rich get richer and the poor get poorer. The rich eat thousands of gold a day and can receive higher education, receiving all material civilization early. The poor are born without the opportunity to receive education. When they are sick, they do not have money to see a doctor, so they just wait to die. In the end, the poor can only die of illness. Then look at the opium prohibition. It is really a good strategy for military and political dignitaries to make profits. Trafficking in opium, shipping opium, smoking opium at home, running rampant and illegally, no one dares to question him. If ordinary people buy a few opium pills to treat stomach pain, once they are discovered, they will be imprisoned for several months and fined. Again, like gambling, ordinary people play cards for entertainment and are arrested by the police station, and they will be fined or beaten with small boards before they can be released. However, military and political dignitaries usually play a few rounds of mahjong, and political expenses and military salaries are sacrificed for their pleasure. As a result, political institutions are in arrears of salaries, and soldiers are in arrears of pay. Who dares to question and punish them? Such a policy of 'only state officials are allowed to set fires, but ordinary people are not allowed to light lamps' makes everyone resentful and indignant, but who dares to say it? We should have a fearless spirit to expose his crimes, like Christ being crucified for the sake of mankind. Secondly, the YMCA itself should be revolutionary and strive for human happiness and sacrifice its own happiness in order to be worthy of being a great Christian youth. We do not need those missionary-style YMCAs and Great World-style YMCAs to exist. I hope all Christian youth will encourage each other to move forward." Mr. Feng's speech lasted about half an hour before it ended.
